< Text>
As other reviews have said, don't judge a book by it's cover. The location is a little sketchy, the shopping center is in need of a facelift and the animal clinic is a little small, but the service was EXCELLENT.
From a referral, I took my cat there for treatment for an abscessed tooth.  Two other clinic‚Äôs quoted me $730 and $575.  I was shocked when the Vet quoted me $120, even included the follow-up antibiotic‚Äôs.

Being a walk-in, I expected a long wait and the typical shuffle routine, but it was surprisingly quick.  While sitting there, I did notice a lapse in attention to the phone, and when they did answer, they were a little short / brief with the customer.  I quess this was due to no Receptionist on duty.  The two Doctors fielded their own calls. That to me was great, speaking directly to the Vet and it keeps the costs down.

Regardless of the price though, I needed to be assured of quality service and care.  My cat normally doesn‚Äôt do well with vet‚Äôs, but was calm throughout the exam, the staff was really nice and seemed very genuine.  The doctor was super great, informative and earnest.  The doctor made me feel completely comfortable leaving our beloved Mojo there.  They had her in an out in only a few hours and everything looked perfectly fine.

Oh, throughout the entire procedure, it was evident that the Doctors were devoted to animals, and the staff were animal lovers. This is a great place that will care for your animals and you won't have to pay an arm and a leg.  I'm so thankful to have found this place!<//Text>

<Text>I had been trying to get some parts for some pro audio gear and had problems with numerous distributors.  At first, I didn't think that this Guitar Center location could help either due to some misunderstandings.  When I visited the store recently regarding this issue, the manager Randy met me at the door.  He was humble, gracious, personable and accommodating.  He even took the time to get to know me, my business and my music background.  This store may have gotten off to a slow start from when they first opened but they have come a long way since.  Their entire staff is knowledgeable and friendly.  The entire Guitar Center corporation has treated me well for decades.  This store is another shining example of their uncompromising professionalism in a sometimes misunderstood and under-appreciated industry.

‚ñ∫‚ñ∫‚ñ∫UPDATE: I have been in the "industry" for many decades.  I never skimp on my own equipment but am hesitant to invest large sums that will be in the hands of customers and guests. <review>Great personalities in the talented people. They are not all that interested in arm twisting - just gentle pointing to answers for your needs. I find the bass department and the live sound people are top-notch; kind and considerate of even the dumbest questions.

I spent a lot of money here in the past few months and they all treat me with the utmost respect from the first time when they didn't know me up until now when I am on a first name business.

I've been to larger GC venues, and they are somewhat more removed from their customers. This Murrietta store is a little smaller and more friendly I feel.
